STEP5: "babbabbbbb" occurs in "adccadccabbba"
applying transition 0 ("babbabbbbb"->"b") gives "-1"
STEP6: "addccabccabccabccabccabccabba" occurs in "-1"
applying transition 4 ("addccabccabccabccabccabccabba"->"") gives "-1"
